## 6. Execution model

Per `docs/spec-authoring-checklist.md` Â¶Ăµ 5, the execution model is declared explicitly:

| Adapter lifecycle | Execution model | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| In-process (`api`, `headless`) | **Inline / synchronous** | Caller blocks on `runAgenticLoop`. Loop result returned by `dispatch()` and consumed by the existing post-completion finalisation block. No queue row. |
| Subprocess (`claude-code`) | **Inline / synchronous** | Caller blocks on `claudeCodeRunner.execute()`. Otherwise identical to in-process. |
| Delegated (`iee_browser`, `iee_dev`, future OpenClaw) | **Queued / asynchronous (pg-boss)** | `dispatch()` returns immediately with `lifecycle: 'delegated'`. Parent agent_run parks in `'delegated'`. Backend's terminal event triggers the shared finaliser. |

This matches today's behaviour precisely. The dispatch ladder is replaced with a registry call; the lifecycle classifications are existing, not new.

The reconciliation cron (`maintenance:backend-reconciliation`) is **queued / scheduled**; it runs every 2 minutes via `boss.schedule()`. Same cadence as today's `maintenance:iee-main-app-reconciliation`.

---

## 7. Refactor mapping Ć’?" existing modes Ć’Ă…' adapters

Each existing dispatch branch becomes one adapter. **No behaviour change.**

| `executionMode` | Adapter file | `capabilities` | `costModel` | `sandboxRequirement` | Lifecycle | Source today |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `api` | `server/services/executionBackends/apiBackend.ts` | `['in_process']` | `'per_token'` | `'none'` | in_process | `agentExecutionService.ts:1522Ć’?"1632` (default branch) |
| `headless` | `server/services/executionBackends/headlessBackend.ts` | `['in_process']` | `'per_token'` | `'none'` | in_process | Same default branch Ć’?" `headless` is a config variant of `api` today; the two adapters share their dispatch implementation via an internal helper, but register as distinct ids |
| `claude-code` | `server/services/executionBackends/claudeCodeBackend.ts` | `['subprocess', 'terminal_repo']` | `'subscription'` | `'terminal_repo'` | subprocess | `agentExecutionService.ts:1474Ć’?"1521` |
| `iee_browser` | `server/services/executionBackends/ieeBrowserBackend.ts` | `['delegated', 'browser_automation', 'cancellation']` | `'per_token'` | `'browser'` | delegated | `agentExecutionService.ts:1413Ć’?"1473` (browser branch of IEE) + `finaliseAgentRunFromIeeRun` |
| `iee_dev` | `server/services/executionBackends/ieeDevBackend.ts` | `['delegated', 'code_execution', 'cancellation']` | `'per_token'` | `'code_execution'` | delegated | Same IEE branch (dev variant) + same finaliser. Sandbox requirement upgrades from collapsed-with-worker to `'code_execution'` once Spec B lands; today the requirement is declared but not enforced. |

#### `api` and `headless` shared body Ć’?" note

The two existing modes share the same physical dispatch path today. The refactor keeps them distinct adapter ids (so `executionMode = 'headless'` resolves correctly) but factors the shared body into an internal helper consumed by both adapter files. This is the only case in V1 where two adapters share code; future adapters get their own files.

#### Migration order (within Phase 2, see Â¶Ăµ 14)

1. Author the contract types + registry (no consumer yet).
2. Land contract tests against an in-memory mock adapter to lock the contract semantics independently of any real adapter.
3. Refactor the IEE adapter first (proven path Ć’?" the existing finaliser + cron + handler are already on the contract's shape).
4. Refactor `claude-code` and `api`/`headless` adapters together (one PR Ć’?" they touch the same file).
5. Switch `agentExecutionService.ts` dispatch from `if/else` to registry call. This is the single cutover commit.

Step 2 (contract tests first) is a hard ordering requirement, not a preference Ć’?" see Â¶Ăµ 17 risk #1.

1. **`loadTerminalState` is used but not in the adapter contract**
- **Section:** Â§4.1, Â§8.2, Â§9.1-Â§9.3
- **Issue:** `finaliseAgentRunFromBackend()` calls `backend.loadTerminalState(...)`, and Â§9.3 says each delegated adapter exposes it, but `loadTerminalState` is absent from the `ExecutionBackend` interface and absent from registry validation. This makes the core finalisation path unimplementable from the declared contract.
- **Suggested fix:** Add to `ExecutionBackend` under delegated lifecycle:
  ```ts
  loadTerminalState?(tx: Transaction, backendTaskId: string): Promise<BackendTerminalState | null>;
  ```
  and update Â§8.2 to require `loadTerminalState` whenever `capabilities` includes `'delegated'`.
- **Severity:** critical

2. **Adapter `finalise()` is described as both pure and DB-writing**
- **Section:** Â§4.1, Â§9.1, Â§13.5
- **Issue:** Â§4.1 says `finalise()` is â€śPure - must not touch DB,â€ť but Â§9.1 says the existing `finaliseAgentRunFromIeeRun` body moves into adapter `finalise()`, and Â§13.5 says `BackendFinalisationResult.finalised` is true only if both rows wrote terminal updates. These cannot all be true.
- **Suggested fix:** Replace the Â§4.1 `finalise()` comment with:
  ```ts
  /**
   * Apply backend-specific terminal mapping and writes inside the caller-owned
   * transaction. May write DB through the provided transaction only; must not
   * open its own transaction or trust event payload data.
   */
  finalise?(input: BackendFinalisationInput & { tx: Transaction }): Promise<BackendFinalisationResult>;
  ```
  Or, if `finalise()` should be pure, move all DB writes explicitly into `finaliseAgentRunFromBackend` and make `finalise()` return only the mapped status/summary/cost projection.
- **Severity:** critical

3. **`preferred_backends` has contradictory runtime semantics**
- **Section:** Â§2 Goals, Â§4.4, Â§8.1, Â§10.3, Â§17 risk #3
- **Issue:** Â§2 says `preferredBackends` is â€śused by adapter resolution as a tie-break,â€ť Â§8.1 says `resolve()` does a lookup â€śplus the preferred-backends override,â€ť but Â§4.4 and Â§17 say V1 identity-resolves / does not use the column at runtime. This leaves implementers unsure whether to build runtime reads and override behavior in V1.
- **Suggested fix:** Pick one. For â€śbuild, do not act on,â€ť change Â§2 goal #6 and Â§8.1/Â§10.3 to:
  ```md
  Add `organisations.preferred_backends` as schema-only forward-compat metadata in V1. `executionBackendRegistry.resolve()` does not read or apply it until Phase 3.5+ routing.
  ```
  If V1 must read it, add the Zod shape and invalid-value behavior now.
- **Severity:** important

4. **`resolve()` is synchronous but is specified to read organisation preferences**
- **Section:** Â§8.1, Â§10.3, Â§12
- **Issue:** `resolve(mode, organisationId): ExecutionBackend` is declared synchronous, but prose says it can read `organisations.preferred_backends`. A DB-backed read cannot fit that signature unless preferences are preloaded, which the contract does not name.
- **Suggested fix:** If preferences are deferred, state:
  ```ts
  resolve(mode: ExecutionMode): ExecutionBackend;
  ```
  and remove the `organisationId` parameter in V1. If preferences are in scope, change to:
  ```ts
  resolve(mode: ExecutionMode, preferredBackends: PreferredBackends): ExecutionBackend;
  ```
  or make it async and name the scoped DB read mechanism.
- **Severity:** important

5. **`executionMode`, `backend_id`, and adapter `id` overlap without a clear source of truth**
- **Section:** Â§3, Â§4.3-Â§4.4, Â§19
- **Issue:** Â§3 says `executionMode` remains the persisted adapter selector, while Â§4.4 adds `agent_runs.backend_id` that equals `executionMode` today but may diverge later. Â§4.3 then uses event `{ backendId, backendTaskId }` to route finalisation. The spec needs a precedence rule for which field wins when `executionMode` and `backend_id` disagree.
- **Suggested fix:** Add to Â§4.3:
  ```md
  Adapter selector precedence: during V1 dispatch, `request.executionMode` is canonical. `agent_runs.backend_id` is a derived snapshot written at dispatch time for delegated reconciliation and trace joins. Finalisation resolves by `backend_id` only for rows already delegated; if `backend_id` is null, the IEE alias path resolves from `iee_runs.task_type`. Divergence between `executionMode` and `backend_id` is invalid in V1 and logged as `backend.selector_mismatch`.
  ```
- **Severity:** important

6. **IEE terminal event payload shape conflicts with existing no-behavior-change claim**
- **Section:** Â§4.3, Â§9.1, Â§11, Â§13.4
- **Issue:** Â§4.3 says event payload contains `{ backendId, backendTaskId }`, while the existing IEE queue is `iee-run-completed` and Â§13.4 says the handler routes by reading `iee_runs.task_type`. Requiring `backendId` in the event payload would change the existing event contract unless the alias path is explicitly preserved.
- **Suggested fix:** Change Â§4.3 to:
  ```md
  Pg-boss event payload is hint only. Generic delegated backends emit `{ backendId, backendTaskId }`. The existing IEE queue keeps its current `{ ieeRunId, ... }` payload in V1; `ieeRunCompletedHandler` loads `iee_runs` and derives `backendId` from `task_type` before calling `finaliseAgentRunFromBackend`.
  ```
- **Severity:** important

7. **Delegated dispatch idempotency does not cover enqueue-then-parent-update partial failure**
- **Section:** Â§4.1, Â§13.1-Â§13.5
- **Issue:** Â§13.1 names the parent `UPDATE ... status IN ('pending','running')` predicate as the idempotency mechanism, but delegated dispatch also enqueues/creates the backend task. If enqueue succeeds and the guarded parent update affects zero rows, the spec does not name the cleanup or reconciliation behavior for the already-created backend task.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a dispatch sequence contract:
  ```md
  Delegated dispatch order: create/enqueue backend task with idempotency key `agent_run:{runId}:{backendId}`, then update parent with `WHERE id = runId AND status IN ('pending','running')`. If the parent update affects zero rows, the adapter must mark the backend task cancelled/orphaned in the same adapter storage and return a diagnostic error; reconciliation must ignore orphaned backend tasks whose parent is already terminal.
  ```
- **Severity:** important

8. **File inventory disagrees on adapter registration file**
- **Section:** Â§11 and Â§18
- **Issue:** Â§11 lists `server/jobs/index.ts` â€śor `server/index.ts` boot blockâ€ť for adapter registration, while Â§18 only lists `server/index.ts`. The â€śorâ€ť leaves the implementation scope ambiguous and violates the inventory as source of truth.
- **Suggested fix:** Replace the Â§11 row with one concrete file:
  ```md
  | Boot registration | `server/index.ts` | Register adapters in registry immediately after the existing IEE handler registration block. |
  ```
  Or add `server/jobs/index.ts` to Â§18 if that is the intended file.
- **Severity:** minor
